📝 Flight Disruption (FD) — gaps the test authors already flagged in the workbook (38)
Testing how agentic is displaying flights with multiple segments when an itinerary has been changed multiple times, example during an IROP - FD-SIT-108
Multi-select flights display in agentic - FD-SIT-109
"Neither" is selected in segment selection - FD-SIT-110
Change in flight info, e.g. "sorry my paris flight not toronto flight" is typed in segment selection - FD-SIT-111
No segment selection path in Miro. We need to test this in the Agentic testing to ensure the right info/ data is being dispalyed - covering by FD-SIT-107
Duplicate claim disputed as it was submitted by someone else - FD-SIT-113
Add YPTU - Please explain what is YPTU expectation in Agentic testing?
Coming back, <72h - FD-SIT-115
Claim submitted more than 1 year from flight disruption - FD-SIT-116
Passenger still waiting for compensation - FD-SIT-117
Are we testing different booking sources? We should. This will not affect agentic testing but other testing - Agree this is only a TT test data creation change only
Should test in different languages - FD-SIT-119
Claiming for both bounds - covering by FD-SIT-109
Appeals to closed cases - FD-SIT-121
Passenger changes intent mid‑conversation after eligibility decision.- FD-SIT-122
Passenger appeals inital FD rejection after moving on to next intent. - FD-SIT-123
Claims company submits but no attachment. - FD-SIT-124
Customer changes language mid conversation. - FD-SIT-125
Disputes currency conversion. - FD-SIT-126
Customer claims for flight disruption and proactive case found for same joruney, pax, etc with non-reg comp issued - FD-SIT-127
Empathy triggered scenarios (weddings, bereavement), will responses adjsut to acknowledge? - FD-SIT-138
Case Status: Customer disputes or asks for update on case while manual case is pending due to customer input needed (ex. agent asks for more info, attachments, IDV, etc) - FD-SIT-139
Customer uses crude language - FD-SIT-140
Customer claims legal action - FD-SIT-141
Customer is not associated to the Aeroplan account on the booking but wants ACW compensation - FD-SIT-142
Deadlocks for EU RegulationsPlease explain this scenarios.

AG Release 5 - Flight Disruption SIT (CHAI-21271)
FD-SIT-001 - APPR eligible - 3 to <6 hour delay - CAD 400 cash
⚙️ Given
⚙️ Is starting a Travel Disruptions / Delays or Cancellations claim from a supported channel.
⚙️ The recognized topic is Travel Disruptions.
⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.
⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.
⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.
⚙️ TripTracer and DDS are available for Flight Disruption assessment.
⚙️ Case Management is available to create, patch, and finalize the case.
⚙️ APPR applies.
⚙️ The disrupted Most Significant Leg is Air Canada operated.
⚙️ The booking is an individual booking, not a group booking.
⚙️ Is a revenue passenger, not youth, not UMNR, and not an infant-excluded case.
⚙️ The disruption is controllable and the customer reaches the promised or sister destination.
⚙️ The applicable wait window has elapsed.
⚙️ CyberSource returns GREEN.
⚙️ No duplicate claim exists.
⚙️ Country of residence is collected and the selected payout rail is available.
When
👤
⚙️ Case Intake creates the shell case with topic Travel Disruptions and sub-topic Delays or Cancellations and stores session context.
⚙️ Eligibility Assessment verifies auth and retrieves TripTracer/DDS context for the selected booking.
⚙️ Eligibility Assessment returns an eligible Flight Disruption result with passengers, bounds, regime, source amount, and source currency.
Selects the passenger and impacted bound.
👤
Case Intake patches the selected passenger, bound, eligibility snapshot, contact details, and source evidence back to the case.
👤
⚙️ Preauth verifies TripTracer fields, duplicate status, wait-window status, fraud-screening status, payout country, payment capability, and payment offer readiness.
⚙️ Is presented with a Flight Disruption compensation offer of CAD 400.
Is shown the Flight Disruption legal disclaimer before accepting
👤
Selects cash payout.
👤
Case Intake collects required payout contact/details and payment-stage IDV succeeds.
👤
Accepts the offer.
👤
Case Intake finalizes the case to submitted_for_processing.
👤
Case Processor picks up the submitted case, confirms compensation and payout readiness, and builds the normalized payment instruction.
👤
Compensation Service routes the payment instruction to IBM cash payout with payment method I.
👤
The provider accepts the payment instruction and returns a provider reference.
👤
The notification trigger runs after successful claim submission.
👤
🤖
Then
🤖
The case reaches submitted_for_processing.
🤖
The approved Flight Disruption compensation amount is CAD 400.
⚙️ No manual-review queue is created.
⚙️ The payment instruction is tracked with provider routing details and callback or reconciliation status.
⚙️ Receives the Air Canada eligible claim summary email.
⚙️ The terminal customer outcome is End Flow.
✅ Expected results from test case

⚙️ Given

⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.


⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.


⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.


TripTracer confirms the customer holds an Aeroplan (FFP) membership number (single passenger; for a multi-pax claim, all claimed passengers)
👤


⚙️ TripTracer and DDS are available for Flight Disruption assessment.


⚙️ Case Management is available to create, patch, and finalize the case.


⚙️ APPR applies.


⚙️ The disrupted Most Significant Leg is Air Canada operated.


⚙️ Is a revenue passenger, not youth, not UMNR, and not an infant-excluded case.


⚙️ The disruption is controllable and the customer reaches the promised or sister destination.


⚙️ The applicable wait window has elapsed.


⚙️ CyberSource returns GREEN.


⚙️ No duplicate claim exists.


⚙️ Country of residence is collected and the selected payout rail is available.


When
👤


⚙️ Case Intake creates the shell case with topic Travel Disruptions and sub-topic Delays or Cancellations and stores session context.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment verifies auth and retrieves TripTracer/DDS context for the selected booking.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment returns an eligible Flight Disruption result with passengers, bounds, regime, source amount, and source currency.


Selects the passenger and impacted bound.
👤

👤

⚙️ Is presented with the compensation methods


Selects AC Wallet as the compensation method
👤


Is presented with a Flight Disruption compensation offer of CAD 480.
👤


Selects AC Wallet payout.
👤


Case Intake collects required payout contact/details and payment-stage IDV succeeds.
👤


Accepts the offer.
👤


Case Intake finalizes the case to submitted_for_processing.
👤


Case Processor picks up the submitted case, confirms compensation and payout readiness, and builds the normalized payment instruction.
👤


Compensation Service routes the payment instruction to IBM cash payout with payment method I.
👤


The provider accepts the payment instruction and returns a provider reference.
👤


The notification trigger runs after successful claim submission.

FD-SIT-005 - APPR eligible - 9 hour or greater delay - CAD 1,000 cash


⚙️ Given


⚙️ Is starting a Travel Disruptions / Delays or Cancellations claim from a supported channel.


⚙️ The recognized topic is Travel Disruptions.


⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.


⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.


⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.

AG Release 5 - Flight Disruption SIT (CHAI-21271)


FD-SIT-007 - APPR eligible - VOL/INVOL promise calculation governs delay


⚙️ Given


⚙️ Is starting a Travel Disruptions / Delays or Cancellations claim from a supported channel.


⚙️ The recognized topic is Travel Disruptions.


⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.


⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.


⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.


⚙️ TripTracer and DDS are available for Flight Disruption assessment.


⚙️ Case Management is available to create, patch, and finalize the case.


⚙️ APPR applies.


⚙️ The disrupted Most Significant Leg is Air Canada operated.


⚙️ The booking has a mix of voluntary (VOL) and involuntary (INVOL) changes.


When
👤


⚙️ Case Intake creates the shell case with topic Travel Disruptions and sub-topic Delays or Cancellations and stores session context.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment verifies auth and retrieves TripTracer/DDS context for the selected booking.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment via EDS sets Promise = last VOL before first INVOL and computes the net delay.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment returns an eligible result reflecting the net delay tier.


Selects the passenger and impacted bound and accepts the cash offer.
👤


Case Intake finalizes the case to submitted_for_processing and Compensation Service routes the payout.
👤


🤖
Then


🤖
The case reaches submitted_for_processing.


🤖
The approved Flight Disruption compensation amount is the net-delay tier amount.


⚙️ No manual-review queue is created.


⚙️ The payment instruction is tracked with provider routing details and callback or reconciliation status.


⚙️ Receives the Air Canada eligible claim summary email.


⚙️ The terminal customer outcome is End Flow.

AG Release 5 - Flight Disruption SIT (CHAI-21271)


FD-SIT-012 - EU 261 eligible - short/medium-haul distance band - EUR 250 / EUR 400


⚙️ Given


⚙️ Is starting a Travel Disruptions / Delays or Cancellations claim from a supported channel.


⚙️ The recognized topic is Travel Disruptions.


⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.


⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.


⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.


⚙️ TripTracer and DDS are available for Flight Disruption assessment.


⚙️ Case Management is available to create, patch, and finalize the case.


⚙️ EU/UK 261 applies.


⚙️ The disrupted Most Significant Leg is Air Canada operated.


⚙️ Is a revenue passenger, not youth, not UMNR, and not an infant-excluded case.


⚙️ The disruption is controllable and the customer reaches the promised or sister destination.


⚙️ The applicable wait window has elapsed.


⚙️ CyberSource returns GREEN.


⚙️ No duplicate claim exists.


⚙️ Country of residence is collected and the selected payout rail is available.


When
👤


⚙️ Case Intake creates the shell case with topic Travel Disruptions and sub-topic Delays or Cancellations and stores session context.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment verifies auth and retrieves TripTracer/DDS context for the selected booking.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment returns an eligible Flight Disruption result with passengers, bounds, regime, source amount, and source currency.


Selects the passenger and impacted bound.
👤


Case Intake patches the selected passenger, bound, eligibility snapshot, contact details, and source evidence back to the case.
👤


⚙️ Preauth verifies TripTracer fields, duplicate status, wait-window status, fraud-screening status, payout country, payment capability, and payment offer readiness.


⚙️ Is presented with a Flight Disruption compensation offer of the distance-band amount (EUR 250 short / EUR 400 medium).


Selects cash payout.
👤


Case Intake collects required payout contact/details and payment-stage IDV succeeds.
👤


Accepts the offer.
👤


Case Intake finalizes the case to submitted_for_processing.
👤


Case Processor picks up the submitted case, confirms compensation and payout readiness, and builds the normalized payment instruction.
👤


Compensation Service routes the payment instruction to IBM cash payout with payment method I.
👤


The provider accepts the payment instruction and returns a provider reference.
👤


The notification trigger runs after successful claim submission.
👤


🤖
Then


🤖
The case reaches submitted_for_processing.


🤖
The approved Flight Disruption compensation amount is the distance-band amount (EUR 250 short / EUR 400 medium).


⚙️ No manual-review queue is created.


⚙️ The payment instruction is tracked with provider routing details and callback or reconciliation status.


⚙️ Receives the Air Canada eligible claim summary email.


⚙️ The terminal customer outcome is End Flow.


✅ Expected results from test case

FD-SIT-020 - APPR and EU/UK 261 both apply - most generous offer displayed


⚙️ Given


⚙️ Is starting a Travel Disruptions / Delays or Cancellations claim from a supported channel.


⚙️ The recognized topic is Travel Disruptions.


⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.


⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.


⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.


⚙️ TripTracer and DDS are available for Flight Disruption assessment.


⚙️ Case Management is available to create, patch, and finalize the case.


⚙️ APPR and EU/UK 261 both apply to the same disrupted trip.


⚙️ The disrupted Most Significant Leg is Air Canada operated.


⚙️ Both regimes return eligible source amounts.


⚙️ Country of residence is collected for payout routing.


⚙️ CyberSource returns GREEN.


⚙️ No duplicate claim exists.


When
👤


⚙️ Case Intake creates the shell case with topic Travel Disruptions and sub-topic Delays or Cancellations and stores session context.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment verifies auth and retrieves TripTracer/DDS context for the selected booking.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment preserves both regime outputs for audit.


⚙️ Preauth presents one most-generous customer offer instead of separate regime outcomes.


Accepts the most-generous cash offer.
👤


Case Processor and Compensation Service process the selected payout instruction.
👤


🤖
Then


🤖
The case reaches submitted_for_processing.


The customer-visible result shows only the selected most-generous offer.
👤


⚙️ No manual-review queue is created.


⚙️ Receives the Air Canada eligible claim summary email.


⚙️ The terminal customer outcome is End Flow.

AG Release 5 - Flight Disruption SIT (CHAI-21271)


FD-SIT-080 - New duplicate found at preauth - controlled handling


⚙️ Given


⚙️ Is starting a Travel Disruptions / Delays or Cancellations claim from a supported channel.


⚙️ The recognized topic is Travel Disruptions.


⚙️ The recognized sub-topic is Delays or Cancellations.


⚙️ Has a valid PNR and last name or supported booking identifier.


⚙️ Completes the required upstream OTP or IDV path for the claim.


⚙️ TripTracer and DDS are available for Flight Disruption assessment.


⚙️ Case Management is available to create, patch, and finalize the case.


⚙️ The booking is an individual booking, not a group booking.


⚙️ The eligibility verdict is available and has been read by Eligibility Assessment (no duplicate existed at EA time).


⚙️ The claim has proceeded past Eligibility Assessment to the Preauth gate.


⚙️ A new duplicate is detected at Preauth


When
👤


⚙️ Case Intake creates the shell case with topic Travel Disruptions and sub-topic Delays or Cancellations and stores session context.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment verifies auth and reads the pre-computed TripTracer/DDS verdict for the selected booking.


⚙️ Eligibility Assessment returns a Flight Disruption result with regime, source amount, and source currency.


Selects the passenger and impacted bound.
👤


Case Intake patches the selected passenger, bound, eligibility snapshot, contact details, and source evidence back to the case.
👤


Preauth runs the duplicate check for the claim.
👤


⚙️ Preauth detects a new duplicate (one that was not present at Eligibility Assessment time).


⚙️ Is offered a choice to close or dispute the duplicate finding.


Selects close (accepts the duplicate finding and does not proceed further).
👤


🤖
Informs the customer that a duplicate claim has been detected.


🤖
Presents the close or dispute choice to the customer.


After the customer selects close, the agent confirms the session has ended without a double case proceeding.
👤


No compensation offer or payment options are presented to the customer.
👤


The terminal customer outcome is End Flow.
👤
